### [106] [LiveSVG: Zero-Shot SVG Animation via Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30174)
*Matan Levy,Ran Margolin,Bar Cavia,Dvir Samuel,Yael Pritch,Shmuel Peleg,Alex Rav Acha,Ariel Shamir,Dani Lischinski*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LiveSVG提出一种零样本从静态SVG生成动画的方法：先用冻结的视频扩散图像到视频模型根据文本提示生成目标视频，再通过可微渲染把原SVG拟合到该视频，结合群组单应与路径控制点偏移实现粗到细运动；引入球堆积重着色解决像素对应；在AniClipart与新建的ChallengeSVG基准上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SVG动画法难以表达复杂非刚性运动：LLM生成代码难以细致操控贝塞尔变形；SDS优化噪声大且常需骨架等先验。需要一种既能对齐文本/视频，又保持SVG可编辑性的通用鲁棒方案。

Method: 输入SVG与运动文本提示：1) 用冻结的image-to-video扩散模型生成可预览的目标参考视频；2) 通过可微矢量渲染，将原SVG拟合到该视频。运动表示为双层：对群组施加单应（捕获关节/大体姿态），对每条路径的贝塞尔控制点做局部偏移（捕获非刚性形变）。为避免颜色导致的像素匹配歧义，提出球堆积式重着色以在拟合期间提升可辨性。无需骨架或类别先验。

Result: 在AniClipart与作者提出的复杂多目标数据集ChallengeSVG上，LiveSVG在对齐度、保真度与可编辑性上显著优于LLM代码生成与SDS类方法，展现稳定、鲁棒的动画生成效果。

Conclusion: 直接将SVG拟合到由扩散模型生成的参考视频是实现提示对齐且可编辑矢量动画的有效路线；双层运动表示与重着色策略关键提升了拟合质量与鲁棒性，并在新基准上验证了先进性。

Abstract: We introduce LiveSVG, a zero-shot approach for generating Scalable Vector Graphics (SVG) animations using video diffusion models. Current SVG animation methods struggle with complex motions: LLM-based code synthesis fails to express fine, non-rigid Bézier deformations, while Score Distillation Sampling (SDS) provides noisy gradients and often requires category-specific priors like skeletons. In contrast, LiveSVG fits vector geometry directly to an explicitly generated target video. Given an input SVG image and a motion prompt, we generate a previewable target video using a frozen image-to-video model, then fit the original SVG to this video via differentiable rendering. Our fitting stage is skeleton-free, utilizing a dual-level motion representation that combines per-group homographies for coarse articulation with per-path Bézier control-point offsets for local deformations. To resolve color-induced correspondence ambiguities during pixel-wise fitting, we introduce a novel sphere-packing recolorization strategy. We also present ChallengeSVG, a benchmark of complex, multi-object scenes that exposes the limitations of prior work. Evaluations demonstrate that LiveSVG significantly outperforms existing methods on both AniClipart and ChallengeSVG, establishing direct reference-video fitting as a practical, robust route to prompt-aligned and fully editable vector animation.

### [107] [Cycle Consistency in Video Object-Centric Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30211)
*Rongzhen Zhao,Zhiyuan Li,Ruonan Wei,Juho Kannala,Joni Pajarinen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出“隐式循环一致性(ICC)”用于自监督视频面向对象学习(OCL)，将循环一致性从槽位特征空间转移到重建流形上，避免特征坍塌并优于显式循环一致性(ECC)基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在MOT中广泛使用的循环一致性在OCL中难以直接应用：OCL的slot表示具有随机性和歧义性，场景分解非唯一；对slot施加显式循环一致性会强迫均值对齐，惩罚同样合理的替代分解，导致特征坍塌。需要一种既能保持时间关联又不抑制多样分解的约束。

Method: 引入隐式循环一致性(ICC)：不在离散/随机的slot潜空间做点对点对齐，而在连续的重建流形上施加一致性约束，让不同时间步的slots对“如何共同重建场景”达成软共识。即通过重建一致性而非特征匹配来传递时间关联，缓解均值寻求。

Result: 在复杂视频OCL基准上，ICC避免了特征坍塌，并在性能上超过施加显式循环一致性(ECC)的基线方法。

Conclusion: 将循环一致性从槽位特征转向重建流形，可在不牺牲多样性与不确定性的前提下实现稳健的跨时关联，提升视频OCL表现并优于传统ECC方案。

Abstract: Self-supervised video Object-Centric Learning (OCL) aims to discover distinct objects and associate them across time, whereas self-supervised Multi-Object Tracking (MOT) focuses on associating pre-defined object detections or segmentations. Although well-established in MOT, Cycle Consistency (CC) cannot naively or explicitly apply to the latent slot space of OCL. Unlike the deterministic and ideal object representations in MOT, OCL slots are inherently stochastic and ambiguous due to non-unique scene decompositions. Enforcing explicit cycle consistency (ECC) on slots imposes rigid mean seeking. This severely penalizes the model for exploring alternative but equally valid decompositions, thereby driving towards feature collapse. To resolve this dilemma, we propose \textit{Implicit Cycle Consistency (ICC)}, which shifts the cycle-consistency constraint from the restrictive slot space to the continuous reconstruction manifold, encouraging slots to reach a soft consensus on collectively interpreting the visual scene rather than forcing rigid point-to-point feature alignment. Extensive experiments on complex video OCL benchmarks demonstrate that ICC avoids feature collapse and outperforms ECC baselines. Our source code, model checkpoints and training logs are provided on https://github.com/Genera1Z/ICC.

</details>


### [108] [Déjà View: Looping Transformers for Multi-View 3D Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30215)
*Alessandro Burzio,Tobias Fischer,Sven Elflein,Qunjie Zhou,Riccardo de Lutio,Jiawei Ren,Jiahui Huang,Shengyu Huang,Marc Pollefeys,Laura Leal-Taixé,Zan Gojcic,Haithem Turki*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DéjàView：使用单一循环Transformer块进行K次显式迭代，实现高效多视角3D重建，参数大幅减少，性能匹配/超越更大前馈模型，并显示循环共享权重带来更强归纳偏置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型前馈式3D重建Transformer参数规模膨胀，而层间操作常近似重复，解码器深度本质上在做逐步细化。作者认为“深度即隐式迭代”，但以独立参数低效实现，因而希望将迭代显式化，提高参数与计算效率并可能带来更好的归纳偏置。

Method: 提出DéjàView：对每个视角的特征，使用同一个Transformer块在时间上循环复用，进行K步细化（recurrent refinement）。训练一次后，K在推理时可调，作为计算旋钮。对比一个参数不共享、每步独立参数的变体，在相同训练数据与计算下评估。

Result: 在五个多视角3D重建基准（室内、室外、物体中心、自动驾驶等）上，DéjàView以远少于对照前馈大模型的参数、相当或更低的计算，达到或超过其性能。循环共享权重版本优于每步独立参数版本。

Conclusion: 将迭代显式化、以单块循环Transformer进行多步细化，不仅是参数/计算更高效的替代方案，还提供更强的结构归纳偏置，推理时可通过K灵活权衡精度与计算，实证优于更大前馈模型与非共享迭代变体。

Abstract: Recent feed-forward 3D reconstruction transformers have scaled to over a billion parameters, following the broader trend of increasing model capacity in computer vision. Yet emerging evidence suggests that contiguous transformer layers often behave like repeated applications of similar operations, and multi-view reconstruction transformers refine their predictions progressively across decoder depth. We posit that model depth partially buys iteration, paid for inefficiently in unique parameters, and instead make that iteration explicit in architecture. Our model, DéjàView, applies a single looped transformer block recurrently to per-view features for K refinement steps. Trained once, it exposes K as an inference-time compute knob, matching or outperforming substantially larger feed-forward baselines across five reconstruction benchmarks spanning indoor, outdoor, object-centric, and driving scenes, while using a fraction of their parameters and comparable or lower compute. Importantly, the same looped block formulation outperforms an otherwise identical variant with independent per-step parameters under matched training data and compute, suggesting that explicit iteration is not merely a compute-efficient substitute for capacity but a stronger inductive bias for multi-view 3D reconstruction.

</details>


### [109] [IP-Adapter Is All You Need: Towards Fine-Tuning-Free Diffusion-Based Talking Face Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30230)
*Hao Wu,Xiangyang Luo,Hao Wang,Jiawei Zhang,Yi Zhang,Jinwei Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种无需微调的扩散式说话人脸生成框架，直接用预训练的Stable Diffusion与IP-Adapter，并配三种“零可训练参数”模块（Structurist、Structure Controller、Noise Sensor）以解决身份漂移、唇同步与时序稳定问题，实验在唇同步与视觉质量上均超越SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以Stable Diffusion+IP-Adapter预训练权重为骨干，利用IP-Adapter视觉嵌入从SD中挖掘与唇相关的语义。设计三个“无需训练参数”的组件：1) Structurist：显式解耦并重组嘴唇与外观特征，缓解身份漂移和外观失真；2) Structure Controller：依据“准单调”的口型运动趋势自适应细化嵌入，提升精确唇同步；3) Noise Sensor：引入高斯先验检测并抑制闪烁/抖动伪影，增强时序一致性。

Result: 在标准基准上优于SOTA：唇同步准确率PCLD提升至少0.16，视觉保真FID提升至少0.7，并展现出稳定、清晰、同步良好的说话人脸生成。

Conclusion: 无需微调的扩散框架可直接复用通用大模型权重，通过结构化控制与先验噪声感知，实现更好唇同步与时序稳定，同时降低计算与数据成本，提升可复现性与可扩展性。

Abstract: With the rapid advancement of diffusion models, talking face generation has made remarkable progress. However, existing diffusion-based methods still require task-specific fine-tuning and large-scale audiovisual datasets, resulting in high computational costs that hinder scalability and accessibility of diffusion-based approaches across the research community. To address this, we propose a finetuning-free paradigm that directly performs talking face generation using the pretrained weights of Stable Diffusion and IP-Adapter. This backbone leverages the visual embedding capability of IP-Adapter to mine lip-related semantics from the pretrained Stable Diffusion. To address the challenges of identity drift, synchronization errors, and temporal instability, we also design three trainable-parameterfree components: (1) the Structurist, which explicitly disentangles and reassembles lip and appearance features to mitigate identity drift and appearance distortion; (2) the Structure Controller, which adaptively refines embeddings based on quasi-monotonic motion trends for precise lip synchronization; and (3) the Noise Sensor, which introduces Gaussian prior to detect and suppress flicker and jitter artifacts and enhance temporal consistency. Experimental results show that our method outperforms existing SOTA approaches in both lip-sync accuracy (at least 0.16 gain in PCLD) and visual fidelity (at least 0.7 improvement in FID), establishing a novel fine-tuning-free diffusion framework for talking face generation.

### [110] [Beyond 3D VQAs: Injecting 3D Spatial Priors into Vision-Language Models for Enhanced Geometric Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30231)
*Chun-Hsiao Yeh,Shengyi Qian,Manchen Wang,Yi Ma,Joseph Tighe,Fanyi Xiao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GASP，在不依赖3D-VQA微调或专用3D编码器的前提下，通过在LLM层内注入几何先验，显著提升VLM的3D空间推理与时序稳健性，并在多项基准上取得大幅领先。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM在3D空间推理上表现脆弱：微调3D-VQA易过拟合数据偏差，接入专用3D编码器又笨重且不灵活。作者主张真正的空间理解应来源于基础几何先验的学习，而非仅依赖高层问答监督。

Method: 提出GASP（Geometric-Aware Spatial Priors）：在LLM的transformer各层引入一个小型对应关系（correspondence）头，作为深度监督信号。使用大规模视频场景的真值几何训练，采用双重目标：1) 基于真值点对应的对比学习，强化跨视角的2D视图不变性；2) 深度一致性监督，缓解/消除3D几何歧义。训练后在层内形成更强的点对应能力与几何表征。

Result: 诊断显示标准VLM的内部点对应匹配准确率<5%。GASP训练后，峰值层内对应准确率>70%，时序鲁棒性>85%，而基线<5%。在下游空间基准显著提升：All-Angles Bench提升+18.2%，VSI-Bench提升+29.0%，且未在任何3D VQA数据上训练。

Conclusion: 将基础几何先验直接注入LLM并以对应与深度一致性双目标训练，可显著改善VLM的内在几何一致性与跨时间稳健性，带来对3D空间推理更可靠、可泛化的能力，避免3D-VQA微调的偏差与专用3D编码器的负担。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) often struggle with robust 3D spatial reasoning. Prevailing methods that rely on fine-tuning with 3D visual question-answering (VQA) datasets may overfit dataset-specific biases, while integrating specialized 3D visual encoders is often inflexible and cumbersome. In this paper, we argue that genuine spatial understanding should emerge from learning fundamental geometric priors, not only from high-level VQA supervision. We propose GASP (Geometric-Aware Spatial Priors), a framework that injects these priors directly into the LLM's transformer layers. GASP employs a small correspondence head, applied as a deep supervision signal across all layers, and is trained with a dual objective leveraging ground-truth geometry from large-scale video scenes: a contrastive loss on ground-truth point correspondences enforces 2D view-invariance, while a depth consistency supervision resolves 3D geometric ambiguities. Our analysis first provides a diagnostic showing that standard VLMs' internal correspondence matching accuracy is very low (often below 5%). We then demonstrate that our training substantially improves this behavior, boosting peak layer-wise correspondence to over 70% and maintaining over 85% temporal robustness while baselines remain below 5%. These internal improvements translate to significant gains on downstream spatial benchmarks including +18.2% on All-Angles Bench and +29.0% on VSI-Bench, all without training on any 3D VQA data. Our findings indicate that learning from fundamental geometric priors is a promising and generalizable pathway towards VLMs with more reliable 3D spatial reasoning.

### [111] [BullingerDB: A Dataset for Handwritten Text Recognition and Writer Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30235)
*Marco Peer,Anna-Scius Bertrand,Patricia Scheurer,Andreas Fischer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BullingerDB 是一个涵盖约2.1万页、近50万行、跨796位书写者、跨六十年的多语种（拉丁语与早期新高地德语为主）历史手稿基准，用于文本识别与书写者检索，并附带作者与时间元信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有历史文献数据集在规模、多语性、长时间跨度与书写者标注方面不足，难以评价随时间变化的风格差异对识别与检索的影响。作者希望提供一个大规模、带时间与作者标注的真实历史语料，以推动多语种文本识别和时间感知的书写者分析研究与评测。

Method: 构建并发布基于海因里希·布林格通信档案的基准数据集（20,898页，499,222行，796位书写者，含作者与时间标签，语言以拉丁语与早期新高地德语为主）。在其上评测文本识别模型（如 TrOCR），并提出面向时间一致性的书写者检索评价指标——temporal nDCG，用于衡量检索结果与时间接近性的匹配程度；同时报告传统检索指标（mAP）。

Result: 在文本识别任务上，TrOCR 达到 9.1% 的字符错误率（CER）。在书写者检索上，引入的 temporal nDCG 显示出可实现时间一致的检索，但整体 mAP 为 78.3%，表明由于长期风格演变带来挑战。

Conclusion: BullingerDB 为多语历史文本识别与时间感知的书写者分析提供了新的大规模基准。尽管可实现一定的时间一致性检索，但跨数十年的风格变化仍显著影响性能，数据集与指标将推动相关方法的发展。

Abstract: We present BullingerDB, a large-scale benchmark dataset for historical document analysis based on the correspondence of Heinrich Bullinger (1504-1575). The corpus comprises 20,898 pages and 499,222 text lines written by 796 writers over six decades, featuring stylistic variation, multilingual content (mostly Latin and Early New High German) as well as meta-information such as writer identity and time. We evaluate BullingerDB on text recognition and writer retrieval. TrOCR, the best performing model, achieves a CER of 9.1%. For writer retrieval, we introduce a temporal nDCG metric to assess time-aware retrieval. While temporally coherent retrieval is achievable, mAP (78.3%) scores indicate challenges due to long-term stylistic variation. With BullingerDB, we aim to establish a new benchmark for multilingual historical text recognition and temporally-aware writer analysis.

</details>


### [112] [SAM3D-Phys: Towards Multi-Object Interactive Simulation in Real World](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30239)
*Xin Dong,Weijian Deng,Lihan Zhang,Tianru Dai,Wenfeng Deng,Yansong Tang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SAM3D-Phys，将多视图重建与生成式3D先验结合，补全被遮挡/缺失的物体几何，并通过物理与外观一致性约束恢复其在场景中的可模拟状态。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 从多视图图像重建场景得到场景几何及物体的部分观测；2) 借助SAM3D生成式先验从部分观测推断完整物体几何；3) 场景一致性恢复：a) 物理约束的空间优化，迭代对齐补全物体至原始位置/姿态；b) 基于掩码的外观蒸馏，用观测图像细化纹理；最终在场景中得到几何完整、姿态与外观一致的干净物体表示。

Result: 能从真实场景重建中恢复可进行物理仿真的完整物体，并在场景内实现多物体、同时、物理一致的交互模拟；生成的物体具有更高的几何完整性、位姿对齐度与纹理保真度。项目页面提供演示。

Conclusion: SAM3D-Phys有效弥补了重建中物体不完整的问题，通过生成先验+物理/外观一致性约束，产出可仿真、可交互的场景内物体表示，为现实场景中的物理交互与仿真提供了实用方案。

Abstract: This work addresses the problem of recovering complete, simulatable object geometry from reconstructed real-world scenes, enabling physics-based interaction with objects embedded in the scene. While modern multi-view reconstruction methods can produce visually accurate environments, objects are often incomplete due to occlusions and limited observations, making them unsuitable for physics simulation. To address this limitation, we propose SAM3D-Phys, a framework that integrates scene reconstruction with generative 3D priors of SAM3D to recover physically simulatable objects. Our approach first reconstructs the scene from multi-view images to obtain scene geometry and partial observations of objects. We then leverage SAM3D to infer complete object geometry from these partial observations. To ensure that the recovered objects remain consistent with the reconstructed scene, we restore scene-consistent object states through two complementary strategies: a physics-constrained spatial optimization algorithm that iteratively aligns the recovered object to its original location, and a mask-guided appearance distillation module that refines texture fidelity based on the observed images. By recovering complete object geometry and restoring its pose and appearance within the scene, SAM3D-Phys produces clean object representations suitable for physics-based simulation, enabling simultaneous and physically consistent interactive simulation of multiple objects within a reconstructed scene. ### [113] [Reinforcement Learning with Robust Rubric Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30244)
*Ya-Qi Yu,Hao Wang,Fangyu Hong,Xiangyang Qu,Gaojie Wu,Qiaoyu Luo,Nuo Xu,Huixin Wang,Wuheng Xu,Yongxin Liao,Zihao Chen,Haonan Li,Ziming Li,Dezhi Peng,Minghui Liao,Jihao Wu,Haoyu Ren,Dandan Tu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出RLR^3：将RLVR从任务级可验证奖励扩展到细粒度“评分标准( Rubrics )”的准则级奖励，结合可验证与不可验证路径、最小暴露、层级聚合与反饱和策略，在15个多模态基准上显著优于RLVR与基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多视觉-语言任务并非完全可由确定性规则验证，往往需要多维度标准（感知细节、推理、约束）来监督；现有RLVR仅适用于可确定验证的任务，Rubrics虽自然适配细粒度监督，但在线RL中其“执行/打分”的可靠性不足，易被模型利用产生假阳性。

Method: RLR^3将样例特定的Rubrics分流：对可验证准则采用“LLM信息抽取器+确定性验证器”；对不可验证准则采用“LLM法官(As-a-Judge)”。为防投机取巧，引入最小暴露策略：对抽取器遮蔽参考答案(ground truth)，对法官遮蔽图像；并用层级聚合强调核心准则优先于附加准则，同时在同批rollout内做抗饱和处理以避免分数顶格。

Result: 在Qwen3-VL-30B-A3B上、15项基准测试中，RLR^3稳定胜过RLVR，整体较基础模型提升约4.7分，并超过官方“指令到思维”模型间的性能差距。

Conclusion: 对部分可验证的多模态任务，准则级的稳健Rubric奖励与最小暴露、层级加权及抗饱和设计，可在保证可核验性的同时显著提升RL效果，并降低可被利用的假阳性；审计实验验证其可靠性提升。

Abstract: While Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is effective for deterministically checkable tasks, many vision-language tasks are partially verifiable, demanding multi-criteria supervision (e.g., perceptual details, reasoning steps, and constraints). Rubrics provide a natural interface for this fine-grained supervision, but their effectiveness depends on the execution accuracy during online RL. We propose Reinforcement Learning with Robust Rubric Rewards ($\text{RLR}^3$), extending RLVR from task-level verification to criterion-level verification. $\text{RLR}^3$ routes instance-specific rubrics through two execution paths: an LLM-as-an-extractor paired with a deterministic verifier, or an LLM-as-a-Judge for non-verifiable criteria. To ensure faithful scoring, $\text{RLR}^3$ introduce a minimal exposure strategy that masks ground truths from extractors and images from judges. Furthermore, $\text{RLR}^3$ employs hierarchical aggregation to prioritize essential criteria over additional criteria, and mitigates score saturation within rollout groups. Evaluated on Qwen3-VL-30B-A3B across 15 benchmarks, $\text{RLR}^3$ consistently outperforms RLVR, yielding a 4.7-point improvement over the base model and exceeding the official instruct-to-thinking model gap. Controlled audits confirm our deterministic verification and minimal exposure significantly reduce exploitable false positives.

### [114] [GenClaw: Code-Driven Agentic Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30248)
*Junyan Ye,Jun He,Zilong Huang,Dongzhi Jiang,Xuan Yang,Rui Chen,Weijia Li*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 设计名为GenClaw的代理式流程：1）检索与推理阶段构建概念与上下文；2）以可执行代码（如SVG、HTML、Three.js）渲染可控的视觉草图；3）调用图像生成模型在草图基础上补充材质、纹理与写实效果。代码作为中间画布，连接语言推理与像素合成。

Result: 在概念到像素的流水线中引入可执行的程序化草图，使系统能精细控制构图与结构，并与生成模型的表达力结合，带来更高的可控性与可解释性。摘要未给出定量指标，但强调实际可控度与工作流可理解性的提升。

Conclusion: 将图像生成从“提示-黑盒合成”转为“推理-代码草图-上色”的分阶段范式，可作为迈向可控、可解释视觉生成系统的重要一步。

Abstract: Image generation models have evolved from text-conditioned pixel synthesis toward multimodal agents endowed with visual comprehension and tool invocation capabilities. Yet, existing agents remain at the mercy of underlying black-box image models. Their workflow is trapped in a repetitive cycle of prompt rewriting for generation refinement, leaving them with no mechanism to directly manipulate the canvas. In essence, the potential of LLMs to serve as a genuine "brush" for precise visual construction remains largely untapped. In this paper, we propose GenClaw, a code-driven agentic image generation paradigm that empowers the agent to create like a human artist: first conceptualizing, then sketching, and finally coloring. Specifically, the agent first constructs the conceptual knowledge and context through search and reasoning. It then utilizes code (e.g., SVG, HTML, Three.js) to render executable visual sketches. Finally, it employs an image generation model to supplement textures, materials, and photorealism. In this workflow, code serves as a controllable intermediate canvas bridging linguistic reasoning and pixel synthesis, seamlessly integrating programmatic logic with the visual expressiveness of generative models. By transforming image generation from a black-box paradigm into a staged process akin to authentic human creation, GenClaw offers a step toward for highly controllable and interpretable visual generation systems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用主动NIR闪光与RGB-NIR相机获取两类数据：受环境光影响的多视角RGB图与受控NIR点光照下的NIR图。设计三阶段逆向渲染流程，融合RGB的外观/颜色信息与NIR在受控照明下的稳定形状线索，联合估计几何与反射率。搭建移动底座上的RGB-NIR相机+NIR闪光主动成像系统，实现密集多视角采集，并构建数据集。

Result: 在多种环境照明场景下，相比现有方法，几何重建更准确、反射率估计更可靠与一致，整体性能显著提升。

Abstract: Inverse rendering aims to reconstruct geometry and reflectance of objects from images. Despite recent progress, existing methods often produces inaccurate reconstructions that are sensitive to ambient illumination conditions. Here we introduce an ambient-robust inverse rendering method enabled by active RGB-NIR imaging. Our key insight is to leverage near-infrared (NIR) flash illumination-imperceptible to human observers-to obtain stable point-light shading that is largely invariant to ambient illumination. By using multi-view RGB images illuminated by ambient light and NIR images acquired with active NIR flash illumination, we reconstruct accurate geometry and reflectance by exploiting the complementary benefits of RGB and NIR images via a three-stage inverse rendering method. To enable dense multi-view acquisition, we develop an active imaging system equipped with a RGB-NIR camera and a NIR flash mounted on a mobile base. Using this system, we collect the first multi-view RGB-NIR inverse rendering dataset captured under multiple ambient illumination conditions. Experiments demonstrate that our method outperforms prior approaches, achieving accurate geometry and reflectance estimation across multiple ambient lighting scenarios.

### [116] [VideoFDB: Evaluating Full-Duplex Vision-Speech Capabilities in Conversational Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30256)
*Amrita Mazumdar,Seonwook Park,Rajarshi Roy,Nikhil Srihari,Shengze Wang,Yuhao Zhou,Julia Wang,Koki Nagano,Shalini De Mello*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出VideoFDB，第一个面向全双工“音视到音视”(AV2AV)对话代理的基准，涵盖真实视频通话中的11类非语言互动动态，提供感知/生成行为分类与基于量表的LM评测框架，揭示现有系统在视觉忽视与字幕化崩溃等系统性失败，并指出级联语音到虚拟人方案无法产生全双工非语言线索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然人机对话是全双工且视听融合，包含持续的言语与非语言信号互动；现有全双工基准仅评估语音，缺少对音视一体的评估，限制了多模态会话体系统的进步。

Method: 构建VideoFDB：1) 收集237段真实双人视频通话片段，覆盖11种非语言会话动态；2) 提出将“感知”与“生成”解耦的行为分类法；3) 设计基于量表、可解释维度的LM-as-judge评估框架，用以衡量非语言会话质量；4) 在开源与闭源视觉-语音代理以及级联语音到虚拟人的系统上进行评测与分析。

Result: 发现系统性失败模式：视觉流被忽视、转为泛化字幕描述（captioning collapse）；当前系统能在显式VQA任务上使用视觉，但在自然对话所需的流式联合音视频对齐/落地方面不足；级联语音→头像系统的架构本质上无法产生全双工非语言信号。

Conclusion: VideoFDB作为首个全双工AV2AV评测基准，为系统化评估与对比分析奠定基础，期望推动下一代多模态会话代理在持续感知与非语言生成方面的进展。

Abstract: Natural human conversation is full-duplex and audio-visual: people simultaneously speak and listen while continuously interpreting and producing nonverbal cues, such as nods, smiles, and gestures. To support successful human-agent interaction, agents must model full-duplex audiovisual conversation; however, existing full-duplex benchmarks evaluate only speech. In this work, we present VideoFDB, the first benchmark to evaluate full-duplex audio-visual-to-audio-visual (AV2AV) conversational agents. VideoFDB contributes (i) 237 dyadic clips spanning 11 nonverbal conversational dynamics from real-world video calls, (ii) a taxonomy separating perception from generation behaviors, and (iii) a rubric-based LM-as-judge evaluation framework with interpretable axes for assessing conversational quality with respect to nonverbal conversational dynamics. Across open- and closed-source vision-speech agents, we find systematic failure modes: captioning collapse and visual-stream ignorance, and we show that current systems exploit vision for explicit visual question answering but not for the streaming joint audiovisual grounding required in natural conversation. We further evaluate cascaded speech-to-avatar systems and find that their architecture fundamentally precludes the production of full-duplex nonverbal cues. As the first benchmark for full-duplex AV2AV interaction, VideoFDB establishes a foundation for systematic evaluation and, we hope, will accelerate the advancement and development of next-generation multimodal conversational agents.

### [117] [Stable-Layers: Fine-Tuning Image Layer Decomposition Models with VLM-Scored Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30257)
*Ciara Rowles,Reshinth Adithyan,Nikhil Pinnaparaju,Vikram Voleti,Mark Boss*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Stable-Layers 通过仅用视觉-语言模型（VLM）反馈，对预训练的图层分解模型进行强化学习微调，无需成对标注。核心是引入两阶段VLM评估（结构化打分＋并列校准）以提供有辨识度的奖励信号，从而稳定GRPO训练，提升图层分离质量并降低重建误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图层分解依赖成对监督或弱监督，成本高且泛化有限；直接用VLM评分作为强化学习奖励会因评分压缩导致方差不足、训练不稳。需要一种无配对监督、又能提供可靠奖励信号的方法来改进图层分解质量。

Method: 以 Qwen-Image-Layered 为基础，采用 Flow-GRPO + LoRA 微调：每图采样多个候选分解，由VLM依据五个编辑相关准则进行结构化逐样本打分；随后在网格式并列展示下让VLM对全部候选重新打分，以校准并扩展评分区分度。利用组内相对优势（GRPO）更新策略，以VLM反馈为奖励进行强化学习。

Result: 在 Crello 数据集上，相比基线模型，Stable-Layers 产生的分解具有更强的图层分离、更少的空白或伪影严重的图层，并实现更低的逐层重建误差。

Conclusion: 通过两阶段VLM评估构造高辨识度奖励，Stable-Layers 能在无配对监督下稳定地用RL提升图层分解质量，证明了VLM引导的RL微调在图像层分解任务中的有效性。

Abstract: We present Stable-Layers, a reinforcement learning framework that eliminates the need for paired supervision by fine-tuning a pretrained layer decomposition model using only feedback from a vision-language model (VLM). Starting from Qwen-Image-Layered, we apply Flow-GRPO with LoRA adaptation, sampling multiple candidate decompositions per image, scoring them with a VLM, and optimising the policy from group-relative advantages. The key challenge lies in designing a reliable reward signal: VLMs scoring samples in isolation tend to compress their judgements into a narrow band, leaving GRPO with little within-group variance to learn from. We address this with a two-stage evaluation pipeline that pairs structured per-sample scoring across five edit-centric criteria with a grid-based calibration step in which the VLM re-scores all candidates side-by-side. Stable-Layers produces decompositions with stronger layer separation, fewer blank or artifact-heavy layers, and lower per-layer reconstruction error on the Crello dataset compared to the base model.

### [118] [minWM: A Full-Stack Open-Source Framework for Real-Time Interactive Video World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30263)
*Min Zhao,Hongzhou Zhu,Bokai Yan,Zihan Zhou,Yimin Chen,Wenqiang Sun,Kaiwen Zheng,Guande He,Xiao Yang,Chongxuan Li,Fan Bao,Jun Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: minWM提出一套从双向视频扩散基础模型出发，将其转化为可控、因果、低时延的实时交互式视频世界模型的全栈开源框架与配套实践。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频扩散模型虽能生成高质量视频，但难以满足交互式“世界模型”的实时性、可控性与因果性需求；缺少从数据到推理的端到端可重复管线。

Method: 提供端到端流程：1) 在双向T2V/TI2V模型上进行相机控制微调；2) 采用Causal Forcing / Causal Forcing++：包含自回归(AR)扩散训练、因果ODE或因果一致性蒸馏、以及非对称DMD；3) 将模型蒸馏为少步自回归生成器以实现低时延滚动；4) 模块化框架，适配多种骨干（如Wan2.1-T2V-1.3B、HY1.5-TI2V-8B，涵盖跨注意力条件注入与MMDiT结构），并可迁移/适配现有世界模型（如HY-WorldPlay）到新数据与延迟目标。

Result: 开源可运行脚本、权重、文档与推理代码；在相机轨迹质量、可控性训练步数、最小batch需求等方面给出实践性消融与经验；实现可摄像机可控、少步、自回归、低延迟的交互式生成。

Conclusion: minWM为构建与适配实时交互式视频世界模型提供可复现、可扩展的配方与工具链，推动从高质视频生成走向可控、因果、实时的世界建模应用。

Abstract: Recent video diffusion foundation models have achieved remarkable progress in high-quality video generation, yet turning them into real-time interactive video world models remains challenging. Interactive world models require controllable, causal, and low-latency rollout, which in practice demands a full pipeline spanning data construction, controllable fine-tuning, autoregressive training, few-step distillation, and streaming inference. In this work, we present minWM, a full-stack open-source framework for building real-time interactive video world models. minWM provides an end-to-end pipeline that converts existing bidirectional T2V/TI2V video foundation models into camera-controllable few-step autoregressive world models. Specifically, minWM first fine-tunes a bidirectional video diffusion model with camera control, and then applies the Causal Forcing / Causal Forcing++ pipeline, including AR diffusion training, causal ODE or causal consistency distillation, and asymmetric DMD, to distill it into a few-step autoregressive generator for low-latency rollout. The framework is modular and architecture-extensible: we instantiate it on representative open backbones, including Wan2.1-T2V-1.3B and HY1.5-TI2V-8B, covering both cross-attention-based condition injection and MMDiT-style architectures. minWM also supports adapting existing video world models, such as HY-WorldPlay, to new data distributions, training recipes, and latency targets. Beyond releasing runnable scripts, checkpoints, documentation, and inference code, we provide practical ablations on camera trajectory quality, controllability training steps, and minimal batch-size requirements. We hope minWM serves as a reproducible and extensible recipe for building and adapting real-time interactive video world models.
  Project Page: [https://github.com/shengshu-ai/minWM](https://github.com/shengshu-ai/minWM)

</details>


### [119] [LoMo: Local Modality Substitution for Deeper Vision-Language Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30265)
*Feng Han,Zhixiong Zhang,Zheming Liang,Yibin Wang,Jiaqi Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文指出现有VLM对“载体替换”（把文本问题换成等价的图片文字）极其敏感，性能大幅下降。作者提出一种轻量的数据策划范式LoMo，通过在单一模态提示中局部把文本片段渲染为图片，构造语义等价的“文本-视觉-文本”序列，促使跨模态表征不变性，从而增强多模态融合与推理能力；在13个基准与多种基础模型上均显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练语料普遍将文本当作查询、图像当作参考，模态分工不对称，导致模型对同一语义在不同载体（文本/图片）上表征不对齐，遇到将文字转成图像（OCR式）输入时性能骤降。需要一种无需改模型、通过数据监督来消除这种“载体敏感性”的方法。

Method: 提出Local Modality Substitution（LoMo）：在训练数据中动态选择局部文本span并将其渲染为图片，形成无缝交错的多模态序列，使同一语义以文本与视觉两种载体同时出现，从而对齐跨模态表征；该范式架构无关、轻量，可直接用于SFT阶段，对多种VLM进行数据层增强。

Result: 在13个多模态基准上验证，LoMo带来一致增益并促进更深的跨模态融合；相较标准SFT，LLaVA-OneVision-1.5-8B提升2.67分，Qwen3.5-9B提升2.82分，其他基座也有稳定改进。

Conclusion: VLM的“载体敏感性”源于语料的模态角色偏置。通过LoMo在数据层施加跨模态不变性监督，可显著提升在载体替换条件下的稳健推理与整体多模态能力，且方法通用、开销小，适合作为训练数据策划的常规组件。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved substantial progress across a wide range of understanding and reasoning tasks, driven by large-scale image-text training aimed at multimodal fusion. Ideally, replacing a textual question with its rendered-image counterpart should leave model performance essentially unaffected. In practice, however, such modality substitution induces dramatic performance degradation. We attribute this "carrier sensitivity" issue to an inherent bias in current training corpora. Across prevalent datasets such as image captioning, VQA, OCR, and web-sourced interleaved data, text and images are typically organized into distinct and asymmetric roles, with text serving as linguistic queries and images as visual references. Such data bias leads VLMs to exhibit distinct preferences for information acquisition across different modalities. Consequently, VLMs fail to align representations of semantically equivalent content across textual and visual carriers, making model reasoning fragile under modality substitution. To address this, we propose Local Modality Substitution (LoMo), a lightweight, architecture-agnostic data curation paradigm designed to provide supervision for cross-modal representational invariance between semantically equivalent text and image carriers. LoMo achieves this by reformulating single-modality prompts into seamlessly interleaved multimodal sequences. It dynamically selects target text spans and recasts them as rendered images, thereby preserving the same semantics across "text, visual, text" carriers. Extensive experiments across 13 diverse multimodal benchmarks demonstrate that LoMo significantly improves overall multimodal reasoning and yields deeper cross-modal fusion. Specifically, it delivers consistent gains across foundational models, improving over standard SFT by 2.67 points on LLaVA-OneVision-1.5-8B and 2.82 points on Qwen3.5-9B.

</details>


### [120] [PhyGenHOI: Physically-Aware 4D Generation of Dynamic Human-Object Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30268)
*Omer Benishu,Gal Fiebelman,Sagie Benaim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出PhyGenHOI：从静态3D人和物（3DGS）出发，结合文本指令生成物理一致、视觉可信的4D人-物交互；通过MDM驱动人体、MPM物理仿真物体，并以3D高斯为统一可微表示，配合对齐、碰撞再仿真与视频SDS三机制提升接触与动量传递效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有4D HOI生成往往忽视真实物理与精确接触，或难以将生成的人体动作与可微物体仿真统一建模；需要在可控文本驱动下，同时保证动作合理、接触准确、动量守恒与外观逼真的方法。

Method: 统一使用3D Gaussian Splats表示人和物；人体由Motion Diffusion Model按文本生成时序动作（语义代理），物体用Material Point Method进行可微物理仿真（物理代理）。三种耦合监督：1）窗口化吸引损失，使人体时空上截获目标物；2）接触驱动的再仿真，在检测到冲击时触发动量一致的再模拟；3）掩模Video-SDS，将视频先验注入接触区域以提升接触保真度。

Result: 在多样人物、物体与动作（如出拳、踢击）上生成物理一致且视觉可信的4D HOI，优于基线；展示了更好的接触对齐与动量传递。

Conclusion: 通过将生成式人体运动与显式物理仿真在统一3DGS表示下深度耦合，PhyGenHOI实现了受文本控制的物理一致4D HOI生成，提供了通用且可微的交互建模框架。

Abstract: We address the task of generating physically accurate and visually faithful 4D Human-Object Interaction (HOI). Given a static 3D human and target object represented as 3D Gaussian Splats (3DGS), our goal is to synthesize dynamic scenes where the human actively engages with the object through actions, such as punching or kicking, in accordance with a given input text. To this end, we introduce PhyGenHOI, a novel framework that couples generative human motion with an explicit physical object simulation. We model the human as a semantic agent driven by a Motion Diffusion Model (MDM) and the object as a physical agent simulated via the Material Point Method (MPM), utilizing 3D Gaussians as a unified, differentiable representation. We supervise their interaction through three coupled mechanisms: (1) A Windowed Attraction Loss that temporally synchronizes generative motion to intercept the object; (2) A Contact-Driven Re-simulation step that triggers physically consistent momentum transfer upon impact; and (3) A Masked Video-SDS objective that injects video-based priors to enhance contact fidelity. Experiments show PhyGenHOI generates physically consistent 4D HOI across diverse actions, humans, and objects, outperforming baselines. Project page and videos: https://omerbenishu.github.io/PhyGenHOI/

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建深度MAP估计框架：对多IQA模型的打分进行先验与似然建模，显式学习每个模型在样本级/分数级的不确定性，从而在后验最大化下得到融合分数；通过细粒度不确定性估计实现对各模型动态加权与抑制；全流程为无监督训练。

Abstract: Over the past decades, numerous Image Quality Assessment (IQA) models have emerged, aiming to predict the perceptual quality of images. However, individual models are often biased toward certain types of image content or distortions, depending on the design principle and process. An intuitive idea is to harness the strengths and mitigate the weaknesses of each IQA model, by fusing the scores of multiple models into a stronger one. Here we make one of the first attempts to seek an optimal solution for the idea and propose a general framework for unsupervised IQA score fusion using deep Maximum a Posteriori (MAP) estimation. The proposed model conducts fine-grained uncertainty estimation at the score level to increase the accuracy and reduce the uncertainty in fused predictions. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate the superiority of the proposed model over individual IQA models and other fusion methods. It also exhibits an interesting capability of rejecting ``bad" models in the fusion process.

### [122] [Grounded 3D-Aware Spatial Vision-Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30307)
*An-Chieh Cheng,Yang Fu,Yatai Ji,Ligeng Zhu,Guanqi Zhan,Zhuoyang Zhang,Zhaojing Yang,Song Han,Yao Lu,Pavlo Molchanov,Vidya Nariyambut Murali,Jan Kautz,Xiaolong Wang,Hongxu Yin,Sifei Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GR3D 是统一的空间视觉语言模型，融合显式/隐式二维指代与单目三维定位，通过在生成中内嵌区域token与区域驱动的3D盒预测，先感知2D再推理3D，显著提升带/不带grounding的空间理解表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM在复杂空间理解与推理上受限：难以在生成过程中精确引用视觉证据，二维到三维的空间映射不足，且缺少将grounding作为归纳偏置来系统增强空间理解的机制。

Method: 提出GR3D：1) 显式2D grounding；2) 隐式2D grounding：在生成时识别实体并将对应区域token内插进文本流，实现“随写随指”；3) 区域提示的单目3D grounding：从已ground的区域查询预测摄像机视角下的3D包围盒，并采用内参感知归一化与稠密几何监督。整体流程为先基于grounded的2D感知再执行3D推断。

Result: 在多种带grounding与不带grounding的空间基准上均有一致提升，显示GR3D的grounding机制能强化VLM的空间理解与推理能力。

Conclusion: 将显式/隐式2D与单目3D grounding统一到一个框架并作为归纳偏置，能显著提升VLM的通用空间理解，且收益超越单纯的grounding任务本身。

Abstract: We present GR3D, a spatial vision language model equipped with three complementary grounding capabilities--explicit 2D grounding, implicit 2D grounding, and monocular 3D grounding--within a single framework. GR3D introduces an implicit grounding mechanism that identifies entity mentions during generation and inserts the corresponding region tokens into the text stream, allowing the model to reference visual evidence on the fly when producing spatial chain-of-thought responses. In parallel, a region-prompted monocular 3D grounding design predicts 3D bounding boxes in the camera view from grounded region queries, supported by intrinsic-aware normalization and dense geometric supervision. Together, these grounding capabilities enable GR3D to decompose complex spatial understanding problems into grounded 2D perception followed by 3D inference. GR3D achieves consistent improvements across grounded and non-grounded spatial benchmarks, demonstrating grounding as an effective inductive bias for strengthening spatial understanding in VLMs. These grounding capabilities collectively enhance general spatial understanding beyond the grounding task itself.

### [123] [City-Mesh3R: Simulation-Ready City-Scale 3D Mesh Reconstruction from Multi-View Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30310)
*Sayan Paul,Sourav Ghosh,Siddharth Katageri,Soumyadip Maity,Sanjana Sinha,Brojeshwar Bhowmick*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: City-Mesh3R提出一套可扩展的端到端图像到网格流程，从大规模无序多视图图像直接重建城市级密闭（三维可水密）网格，避免传统全局SfM+稠密重建的高复杂度与不规则噪声表面问题，并通过分治、拓扑聚类、几何感知相机选择与曲率自适应重网格，实现高保真、规则、可模拟的城市级三维模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于NeRF/高斯点云等方法在城市尺度上常产生不完整/噪声几何，难以得到可用于仿真的水密网格；而将小规模传统重建方法简单扩展到超大场景计算代价过高。需要一种既可扩展、又能直接产出规则水密网格的解决方案。

Method: 采用分而治之的端到端images-to-mesh框架：1) 通过拓扑图像聚类进行簇内独立稀疏SfM与地图合并，避免穷举特征匹配，得到稀疏城市地图；2) 对地图进行空间划分，执行几何感知的相机选择；3) 在各分区进行稠密表面重建与基于曲率的自适应顶点密度重网格（表面细化）；4) 将各分区网格缝合，形成全局城市网格。

Result: 在城市级数据集上，实现高保真、水密、几何规则且能捕获细节的三维网格；在定性与定量评测中表现优异，并能在分布式设置下扩展到任意大场景。

Conclusion: City-Mesh3R通过拓扑聚类+几何感知选择+曲率自适应重网格的分布式端到端流程，有效解决城市尺度三维重建的可扩展性与网格质量问题，产出适用于下游仿真的水密高质量城市网格。

Abstract: City-scale 3D surface reconstruction from multiview images for downstream 3D simulation, poses highly challenging problems due to the scale and complexity of urban scenes. Existing city-scale 3D reconstruction methods based on NeRF, Gaussian Splatting etc. often fail to recover 3D meshes ready for simulation due to incomplete/missing geometry and irregular, noisy surfaces. Scaling existing small-scale 3D reconstruction methods to arbitrarily large urban scenes is highly infeasible due to their computational complexity. We present City-Mesh3R, a scalable framework for reconstructing watertight surface meshes directly from large unordered image collections. Unlike recent methods which use global sparse SfM point-cloud initialization followed by a distributed 3D dense reconstruction of large-scale scenes, our method follows an end-to-end images-to-mesh 3D reconstruction approach using a divide-and-conquer strategy. The sparse city map is reconstructed via topological image clustering, cluster-wise independent sparse SfM and map merging, without need for exhaustive image feature matching. Then this map is partitioned spatially to perform geometry-aware camera selection, followed by dense surface reconstruction and surface refinement using curvature-aware adaptive vertex density remeshing. These partition meshes are then stitched together to produce the global mesh of the city. The proposed end-to-end framework is evaluated on city-scale reconstruction datasets. As demonstrated by our qualitative and quantitative results, our proposed method yields high-fidelity watertight 3D meshes with regular geometry, capturing fine surface details, and is suitable for scaling to arbitrarily large scenes owing to the end-to-end processing in a distributed setting.

</details>


### [124] [Archon: A Unified Multimodal Model for Holistic Digital Human Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30311)
*Chong Bao,Shichen Liu,Lijun Yu,David Futschik,Stylianos Moschoglou,Shefali Srivastava,Ziqian Bai,Feitong Tan,Guofeng Zhang,Zhaopeng Cui,Sean Fanello,Yinda Zhang*

TL;DR: 提出Archon：一个面向数字人、可统一生成文本/音频/动作/视觉等七种模态的全预训练自回归模型，并配合语义视频再参数化与语义驱动扩散解码器，实现高保真、可控、端到端的数字人生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 统一框架：为七种模态设计专用tokenizer，并用同步数据预训练一个原生自回归统一模型，联合建模72类任务的多模态分布。2) 语义视频再参数化：将高维视频token压缩为语义紧凑表示，约4倍token削减，同时通过语义驱动的视频扩散解码器恢复细节。3) “按模态思考”（Thinking in Modality）：将含糊的跨模态任务分解为跨模态链式推理，逐步提升保真与可控性。

Result: 在多种数字人生成任务（含文本转语音/动作/视频、语音驱动表情与口型、跨模态编辑与组合等）上，实验显示性能优于或可比于当前方法；在高保真说话视频上，以更少token维持细粒度动态与画质；跨模态控制的稳定性与一致性提升。

Abstract: Digital humans are fundamental to immersive interaction, yet creating a unified model for holistic modalities, including text, audio, motion, and visual content, remains an open challenge. In this paper, we present Archon, a fully pretrained, human-centric unified multimodal model for holistic avatar generation. Archon unifies seven modalities with modality-specific tokenizers, and a native autoregressive unified multimodal model pretrained on synchronized modalities and 72 diverse tasks to model holistic joint distributions. To address the token explosion challenge in high-fidelity talking videos, we introduce a memory-efficient semantic video reparameterization, achieving 4x token reduction while preserving fine-grained dynamics, coupled with a semantic-driven video diffusion decoder. We further propose a "Thinking in Modality" that decomposes ambiguous cross-modal tasks into stepwise thinking in an alternative chain of modality, progressively enhancing fidelity and controllability. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Archon achieves superior or comparable performance across diverse digital human generation tasks, validating the effectiveness of our unified framework. Project page: https://zju3dv.github.io/archon/.

### [125] [VPG: Visual Prefix Guidance for Autoregressive Image and Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30317)
*Xinyao Liao,Qiyuan He,Yicong Li,Jiayin Zhu,Xiaoye Qu,Wei Wei,Angela Yao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种训练无关、推理时使用的引导方法VPG，通过对比“真实生成前缀”和“扰动前缀”的模型输出并外推logits，从而缓解自回归图像/视频生成的曝光偏置与前缀漂移，提升图像与视频生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归图像/视频生成在训练用教师强制的真实历史，但推理需依赖自身生成的前缀，容易因误差累积导致曝光偏置与前缀漂移。现有方法多需改训练或仅对外部条件（标签/文本）做采样引导，缺乏直接评估“下一步预测是否增强对已生成前缀的后验支持”的机制。

Method: 提出Visual Prefix Guidance（VPG），在推理时：1）给定当前生成的前缀，计算模型的下一步输出分布；2）构造一个经腐化/扰动的前缀，计算其对应的输出分布；3）对两者进行对比，沿着能提高对原始前缀后验一致性的方向外推logits，偏置采样到能加强前缀支持的候选；无需再训练基础模型。

Result: 在三类任务上验证：类条件图像生成（VAR）、文生图像（Infinity）、文生视频（InfinityStar）。VPG在无需再训练的前提下提升质量：在VAR上平均FID下降0.36，并在多项图像与视频基准上取得更好表现。

Conclusion: VPG作为一种训练无关的推理期引导，直接以“对生成前缀的后验支持”为目标来调整下一步预测，能缓解曝光偏置与前缀漂移并稳定自回归生成，在不同任务和模型上带来一致增益。

Abstract: Autoregressive image and video generators are trained with teacher-forced histories but must sample from their own generated prefixes at inference time, making them vulnerable to exposure bias and prefix drift. Existing remedies either modify training or apply sampling-time guidance aimed primarily at external semantic conditions, such as class labels or text prompts, rather than testing whether a next-step prediction provides strong posterior support for the generated prefix itself. We propose Visual Prefix Guidance (VPG), a training-free inference-time guidance method for autoregressive image and video generation. VPG improves next-step prediction by contrasting the model's output under the generated prefix with its output under a corrupted prefix, then extrapolating logits toward candidates that strengthen the posterior support of the generated prefix. Across class-conditional image generation with VAR, text-to-image generation with Infinity, and text-to-video generation with InfinityStar, VPG improves generation quality without retraining the base model, reducing FID on VAR by 0.36 on average and improving benchmark performance on both image and video generation.

</details>


### [126] [MonoPhysics: Estimating Geometry, Appearance, and Physical Parameters from Monocular Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30320)
*Daniel Rho,Jun Myeong Choi,Matthew Thornton,Biswadip Dey,Roni Sengupta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MonoPhysics在单目视频下联合优化几何、外观与物理参数，凭借三座“视觉-物理桥梁”缓解尺度与几何歧义，使单目性能接近多视角方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 逆物理通常依赖多视角几何约束解决尺度与3D结构，但单目场景缺乏跨视角约束，导致尺度不确定、几何误差大、外观与物理弱耦合，需要一种仅用单目观测也能稳健恢复可变形体物理参数的框架。

Method: 提出MonoPhysics：将可微MPM仿真与3D Gaussian Splatting融合，端到端从单目视频联合优化几何、外观和物理参数。核心是三条视觉-物理桥梁：(1) 全局尺度对齐，解决单目尺度模糊；(2) 面向物理的几何细化，用仿真反馈修正重建形状；(3) 可微位置映射，使像素与仿真网格/粒子位置可微耦合，增强渲染-仿真一致性。

Result: 在Vid2Sim与新建弹塑性数据集上，单目设置下优于现有基线；仅用单目即可达到与多视角基线相当的性能。

Conclusion: 通过三种视觉-物理桥梁与可微渲染+仿真联合优化，MonoPhysics在无多视角约束的单目条件下可靠地恢复可变形体物理属性与几何外观，并缩小与多视角方法的性能差距。

Abstract: Existing inverse physics methods recover physical parameters from multi-view videos, where geometric constraints across views resolve scale and 3D structure. In monocular settings, however, such constraints are absent, leading to severe scale ambiguity, inaccurate geometry, and weak coupling between appearance optimization and physical simulation. We propose MonoPhysics, a framework for monocular inverse physics estimation of deformable objects using differentiable MPM simulation and 3D Gaussian Splatting, which jointly optimizes geometry, appearance, and physical parameters from a single camera view. We address these challenges through three visual-physical bridges: global scale alignment, physics-aware geometry refinement, and a differentiable position map, which together enable accurate optimization from monocular observations alone. We evaluate on Vid2Sim and our new dataset of elastic and plastic objects, showing that MonoPhysics outperforms existing baselines in monocular settings and achieves performance comparable to multi-view baselines using only a single camera. Our project page is available at https://daniel03c1.github.io/MonoPhysics/

### [127] [Veda: Scalable Video Diffusion via Distilled Sparse Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30325)
*Shihao Han,Hao Yang,Xinting Hu,Xiaofeng Mei,Yi Jiang,Xiaojuan Qi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Veda 提出一种与全注意力“瓷砖式(tile-wise)”几何对齐的稀疏注意力框架，通过面向重建的瓦片选择与硬件高效的跳过内核，将极高稀疏度转化为实际加速，在大视频扩散模型中实现显著提速且几乎无画质损失。

Method: 把瓦片选择视为从全注意力重建的显式问题，提出Veda：1) 统计感知的瓦片打分以降低估计误差；2) 头感知的瓦片划分以减少结构失配；3) 硬件友好的tile-skipping算子将理论稀疏度转化为端到端加速。

Result: 在Waver与Wan2.1等大规模视频扩散模型上，无明显画质劣化前提下显著加速：以Waver-T2V-12B生成720P 10秒视频为例，端到端加速5.1×，自注意力加速10.5×，注意力开销由92%降至50%；且序列更长时收益更大。

Conclusion: 决定质量的不是稀疏率本身，而是稀疏掩码与全注意力块几何的一致性。Veda通过重建驱动的瓦片选择和硬件优化，实现可扩展的高稀疏度注意力，在更高时空分辨率下具有更优的可扩展性与实际加速。

Abstract: Scaling Diffusion Transformers to generate high-resolution, long videos is constrained by the quadratic cost of self-attention, and existing sparse attention methods degrade under high sparsity. We show empirically that generation quality is determined not by the sparsity ratio itself, but by how well the sparse mask aligns with the tile-wise geometry of full attention. Based on this insight, we propose Veda, a distilled sparse attention framework that formulates tile selection as an explicit reconstruction problem from full attention. Veda integrates statistics-aware tile scoring with head-aware tiling to reduce estimation error and structural mismatch, enabling aggressive sparsity. A hardware-efficient tile-skipping kernel converts theoretical sparsity into practical wall-clock speedups. Experiments on large video diffusion models, including Waver and Wan2.1, demonstrate substantial acceleration with no noticeable degradation in generation quality. To generate 720P 10-second videos on Waver-T2V-12B, Veda achieves a 5.1$\times$ end-to-end speedup and a 10.5$\times$ self-attention speedup, reducing attention overhead from 92% to 50%. Notably, the gains increase with sequence length, indicating that Veda scales favorably with spatiotemporal resolution across models.

Abstract: Efficient and robust 3D scene representation is crucial in autonomous driving, robotics, and related fields. Lately, novel view synthesis methods like 3D Gaussian Splatting have started using multiple modalities to further boost their performance. It also reduces the training time significantly, by 12 mins 47 secs (55% improvement). Overall, our method is successful in deriving these thermal radiance fields, which can ultimately have several applications, such as identifying heat sources critical in surveillance, search or rescue operations, and industrial inspections where temperature is widely used to monitor machines.

### [129] [Colored Noise Diffusion Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30332)
*Hadar Davidson,Noam Issachar,Sagie Benaim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种在扩散采样中注入“有色噪声”的推断方法CNS，用频率与时间步自适应地分配噪声能量，匹配扩散模型先低频后高频的谱偏置，从而在不改训练的情况下显著提升生成质量与FID。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型生成过程存在“先全局低频、后细节高频”的谱偏置，但现有SDE求解器在整个轨迹中均匀注入白噪声，忽视频率动态，导致能量预算使用低效、偏离数据流形。需要一种与频率解耦、面向未解析结构的能量调度策略。

Method: 将SDE推断重解释为“频率解耦的能量转移”问题，依据模型在各时间步对不同频段的解析程度，设计时间步与频率联合依赖的噪声注入日程：对未解析的频段分配更多能量、对已解析的频段减少注入；由此得到无需再训练、可即插即用的Colored Noise Sampling（CNS）随机求解器，替换常规模型的采样器。

Result: 在多种架构（SiT、JiT、FLUX）与数据集上，CNS作为推断期替换件优于标准ODE/SDE基线：例如ImageNet-256无引导下FID显著下降——SiT-XL/2从8.26到6.27，JiT-B/16从32.39到26.69，JiT-H/16从11.88到8.31；与CFG结合时也有稳定的相对改进。

Conclusion: 利用扩散模型的谱偏置，通过频率与时间步自适应的有色噪声注入，可更高效地把生成分布推向真实数据流形；CNS无需再训练、可即插即用，并在多架构上带来一致的FID收益。

Abstract: Diffusion models achieve state-of-the-art image synthesis, with their generative trajectories fundamentally exhibiting a spectral bias, resolving low-frequency global structures early and high-frequency fine details later. Conventional stochastic differential equation (SDE) solvers fail to account for this dynamic, naively injecting uniform white noise throughout the entire process and misusing the finite energy budget. In this work, we establish a mathematical framework that reconsiders SDE inference as a targeted, frequency-decoupled energy transfer. Leveraging this framework, we introduce Colored Noise Sampling (CNS), a novel, training-free stochastic solver. Rather than injecting uniform white noise, CNS utilizes a dynamic, timestep- and frequency-dependent schedule that more efficiently allocates injected energy toward structurally unresolved frequency bands. By actively exploiting the model's inherent spectral bias, CNS systematically steers the generated distribution toward the true data manifold. Extensive experiments demonstrate that CNS significantly outperforms standard ODE and SDE baselines as a strictly plug-and-play, inference-time sampler substitution across diverse architectures (SiT, JiT, FLUX). Compared to standard sampling on ImageNet-256, CNS achieves substantial unguided FID reductions, improving from 8.26 to 6.27 on SiT-XL/2, 32.39 to 26.69 on JiT-B/16, and 11.88 to 8.31 on JiT-H/16, while yielding consistent relative FID improvements with Classifier-Free Guidance. Project page is available at https://hadardavidson.github.io/CNS/.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 REST3D：1) 代理式物理场景理解，构建以重力支撑为核心的场景树，编码物体物理状态与相互支撑/接触关系，作为结构先验；2) 使用图像到3D模型进行初始重建；3) 基于场景树的引导对齐；4) 在保持与输入图像视觉一致性的同时进行物理约束优化，修正悬空、穿透等物理违规。

Conclusion: REST3D 将物理结构理解与约束优化融入单图重建，可生成仿真可用且与输入图像一致的3D场景，为沉浸式交互与内容创作提供更可靠的资产。

Abstract: Reconstructing physically stable 3D scenes from a single RGB image enables casual images to be converted into simulation-ready digital assets for applications such as immersive interaction and content creation. However, existing single-image reconstruction methods fall short in capturing the physical structure of a scene. As a result, they often produce geometrically plausible but physically inconsistent results, including object floating and penetration, which lead to unstable behavior in physics simulations. Image-conditioned scene generation methods improve physical plausibility but often rely on strong scene priors, yielding plausible yet inaccurate object arrangements that fail to match the input image. We propose REST3D, a single-image reconstruction framework that can reconstruct physically stable 3D scenes by integrating physical scene understanding with physics-constrained refinement. We first introduce an agentic physical scene understanding technique that constructs a scene-tree representation capturing object physical states and inter-object relationships from a gravity-support perspective, providing a structural prior for reconstruction. Leveraging this structure, we initialize the scene using image-to-3D models, followed by scene-tree-guided alignment and physics-constrained optimization to resolve physical violations while preserving visual consistency with the input image. Experiments show that our method significantly reduces physical errors and improves simulation stability on both synthetic and real-world datasets while maintaining strong reconstruction quality. We further demonstrate the reconstructed scenes in VR-based human-object interaction, showing their potential for immersive applications.

Abstract: Generative video-to-audio (V2A) models produce highly plausible soundtracks, but it remains unclear whether they capture the underlying physical processes. Existing evaluations emphasize perceptual realism and overlook physical correctness under controlled interventions. In this paper, we introduce FlatSounds, a benchmark that audits the physical reasoning of V2A models through: 1) controlled counterfactual pairs in which a single physical factor is varied, and 2) single-video pattern tests that probe internal consistency and directional trends. These settings test whether the generated audio correctly reflects specific physical properties and timings. Our evaluation of state-of-the-art models reveals a consistent trade-off: models rely more on text captions than the visual stream to infer physics and semantics. Captions generally improve physical and semantic accuracy, but paradoxically degrade temporal alignment. Our results highlight the need to move beyond audio quality toward learning physical processes directly from pixels. Finally, we find that our physics-based metrics correlate strongly with human preference tests on our own data. Project webpage: https://research.nvidia.com/labs/cosmos-lab/flatsounds/

### [133] [Uncertainty-driven 3D Gaussian Splatting Active Mapping via Anisotropic Visibility Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30342)
*Shangjie Xue,Jesse Dill,Dhruv Ahuja,Frank Dellaert,Panagiotis Tsiotras,Danfei Xu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GAVIS：在3D Gaussian Splatting中用各高斯粒子相对训练视角的各向异性可见度场（球谐表示）来估计不确定性，并将其融入贝叶斯渲染器，实现实时不确定性评估与基于信息增益的主动建图，精度与效率均优于以往且可后处理提升现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在训练未覆盖或少观测区域的合成视图预测不可靠，现有方法缺少对“从哪些视角可见/不可见”的显式建模与高效不确定性量化与主动探索策略，需要一个既物理动机明确又可实时的可见度与不确定性框架。

Method: 1) 定义可见度场：对每个高斯粒子，相对训练视角的各向异性可见度，用球谐函数紧凑表示；2) 将可见度场嵌入不确定性感知的3DGS栅格化渲染器，以贝叶斯网络形式传播不确定性，实现约200FPS的实时不确定性估计；3) 在最大信息增益框架下进行主动建图/视角选择；4) 方法可作为后处理集成到现有3DGS/相关方法中。

Result: 在多样场景的广泛实验中，GAVIS在重建与渲染质量、不确定性校准、以及主动建图效率上均显著优于现有方法，并保持实时速度（约200FPS）；作为后处理也能提升已有方法性能。

Conclusion: 显式建模各向异性可见度并与贝叶斯渲染耦合，可在3DGS中高效、准确地量化不确定性并驱动主动探索；GAVIS提供了统一、可实时的框架，兼具更好精度与更高效率，且具有良好兼容性与扩展性。

Abstract: We present Gaussian Splatting Anisotropic Visibility Field (GAVIS), a novel framework for uncertainty quantification and active mapping in 3DGS. Our key insight is that regions unseen from the training views yield unreliable predictions from the 3DGS. To address this, we introduce a principled and efficient method for quantifying the visibility field in 3DGS, defined as the anisotropic visibility of each particle with respect to the training views, and represented using spherical harmonics. The resulting visibility field is integrated into a Bayesian Network-based uncertainty-aware 3DGS rasterizer, enabling real-time (200 FPS) uncertainty quantification for synthesized views. Active mapping is further performed within a maximum information gain framework building on this formulation. Extensive experiments across diverse environments demonstrate that GAVIS consistently and significantly outperforms prior approaches in both accuracy and efficiency. Moreover, beyond standalone use, our method can be applied post-hoc to improve the performance of existing approaches.

### [134] [YoCausal: How Far is Video Generation from World Model? A Causality Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30346)
*You-Zhe Xie,Yu-Hsuan Li,Jie-Ying Lee,Kaipeng Zhang,Yu-Lun Liu,Zhixiang Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: YoCausal 提出一个基于真实视频、零成本时间反转的两级评测，用于检验视频扩散模型是否具备因果理解而非仅拟合时序统计；引入RSI评估时间箭头感知，CCI结合VLM区分因果/非因果以测因果认知；对13个SOTA模型评估显示，感知时间箭头≠因果理解，人机差距显著。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有因果评测多为合成数据，存在显著的仿真到真实鸿沟；VDM被寄望为世界模型，但尚不清楚其是否真正具备因果推理能力而非仅捕捉时序相关性。需要一个可扩展、基于真实世界且成本低的基准来区分“时间方向感知”和“因果认知”。

Method: 提出YoCausal，两级设计：1) 利用真实视频及其时间反转作为天然反事实样本；定义反转惊讶指数RSI，用扩散模型去噪损失差异量化时间箭头感知。2) 引入大视觉语言模型（VLM）对数据进行因果/非因果分层，构建因果认知指数CCI，从而将真正的因果推理与纯时序偏置分离。评测13个SOTA视频扩散模型。

Result: 实验发现：多数模型能在一定程度上通过RSI感知时间箭头，但在CCI衡量的因果认知上表现显著不足；感知时间方向并不等同于理解因果，且与人类水平存在明显差距。

Conclusion: YoCausal为评估VDM因果能力提供了可扩展、现实世界友好的框架；结果强调当前VDM仍缺乏真正的因果理解，应推动模型与训练策略从时序统计拟合转向因果结构学习。

Abstract: As video diffusion models (VDMs) advance toward world models, a key question arises: do they truly understand causality, or merely overfit to statistical temporal patterns? Existing benchmarks mostly rely on synthetic data, limiting real-world generalization due to the sim-to-real gap. We present YoCausal, a two-level benchmark inspired by the Violation of Expectation (VoE) paradigm from cognitive science. By temporally reversing real-world videos at zero cost as natural counterfactual samples, YoCausal establishes an arbitrarily extensible evaluation protocol. Level 1 introduces the Reverse Surprise Index (RSI), quantifying arrow-of-time perception via denoising loss. Level 2 introduces the Causality Cognition Index (CCI), which leverages a VLM to stratify datasets into causal and non-causal subsets, disentangling genuine causal reasoning from temporal bias. Evaluation of 13 state-of-the-art VDMs reveals that perceiving the arrow of time does not imply understanding causality, and a significant gap persists relative to human-level causal cognition.

</details>


### [135] [NeuROK: Generative 4D Neural Object Kinematics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30347)
*Chen Geng,Guangzhao He,Yue Gao,Yunzhi Zhang,Shangzhe Wu,Jiajun Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出NeuROK：学习物体中心的潜在运动学表征，用于在低维潜空间内进行物理一致的4D动态生成，较传统基于显式物理建模的方法更通用、可扩展且效果更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有4D动态生成多依赖预设物理模型与参数辨识，导致方法受限于特定类别、小规模数据，难以在大规模、跨类别场景下生成逼真的时变形变。需要一种数据驱动、通用且可扩展的表示来替代手工物理建模。

Method: 学习“神经对象运动学”(NeuROK)：以变换器编码-解码器在大规模4D数据上同时学习（1）潜在状态空间，表示物体可能出现的全部动力学/形变状态；（2）解码器，将任意潜在向量映射为该物体的可行形变几何。随后在该低维潜空间内，从拉格朗日力学视角建模与求解动力学，从而简化仿真与生成。

Result: 在多类动态对象上进行实验，NeuROK展现出比既有方法更好的通用性与生成质量，能稳定产生物理可解释、时序连贯的4D形变；与基线相比有明显性能优势（定性/定量）。

Conclusion: 通过学习对象中心的低维运动学潜表示并在其上进行动力学建模，可显著简化4D仿真生成，突破基于预设物理模型的限制，具备跨类别、可扩展与高质量生成能力。

Abstract: Data-driven approaches have revolutionized 3D vision, enabling transformers to effectively reconstruct and generate static 3D objects. However, generating simulative 4D dynamics -- realistic temporal deformations of static objects under various physical conditions -- remains challenging and often ad hoc, despite its importance in building comprehensive 3D world models. Most existing methods assume a predefined physical model and use system identification to estimate parameters, restricting these methods to specific categories and small-scale datasets. We propose that these restrictions can be overcome by learning a data-driven kinematic state parameterization for object-centric physical systems. Specifically, we learn both a latent space representing all possible states of the object and a decoder that maps any sampled latent to a plausibly deformed shape of the object. We refer to this parameterization as Neural Object Kinematics (NeuROK), and learn a transformer-based encoder-decoder model on a curated large-scale 4D dataset. This formulation and the learned model significantly simplify the generation of simulative dynamics since we only need to consider the dynamics within a low-dimensional latent space from the Lagrangian mechanics' perspective in classical physics. We demonstrate the effectiveness and generality of this neural simulation framework across diverse dynamic object types, showing clear advantages over prior works. Project page: https://chen-geng.com/neurok

</details>


### [136] [AdaState: Self-Evolving Anchors for Streaming Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30349)
*Yusuf Dalva,Pinar Yanardag*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出在自回归视频扩散中，用“自适应状态”取代固定首帧锚点，显著增强运动与场景推进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自回归视频扩散顺序生成并强依赖首帧，其KV缓存中首帧成为最干净的注意力锚点，导致模型过度关注静态一致性，抑制运动、机位变化与剧情推进，视频时间维度变浅。

Method: 在每个生成块同时去噪一个不可见的隐藏“状态”向量（不渲染），作为动态场景锚点。模型在每步通过注意前一状态与当前内容生成新的状态；时间被视为相对的：每步拥有同构的位置结构、同一的状态转移。去噪过程即为递推的转移函数，KV缓存承载递推，无需外部模块。

Result: 实验显示采用自适应状态后，视频的运动更丰富、机位与场景演化更自然，整体动态表现显著提升。

Conclusion: 用可递推的自适应隐藏状态替代静态首帧锚点，可缓解时间浅化与过度静态一致性问题，提升自回归视频扩散的时序动态与场景推进质量。

Abstract: Autoregressive video diffusion models generate streaming video by producing frames sequentially, conditioning each chunk on previously generated content. These models are structurally anchored to the first frame: its key-value representation occupies a privileged position in the attention cache and serves as the primary scene reference throughout generation. As the cleanest and most error-free position in the cache, this anchor draws disproportionate attention, suppressing video dynamics, and locking scene composition to the initial viewpoint even as the scene naturally evolves. The result is a temporally shallow video in which motion, camera movement, and scene progression are dampened in favor of static consistency. To address this, we replace the static anchor with an adaptive state, a hidden latent that the model denoises alongside content at every chunk but never renders. Rather than referencing a frozen first frame, the model generates its own scene anchor at each step by attending to both the previous state and the current content, producing a reference that evolves with the generated content. Unlike standard video generation, which encodes an absolute notion of time, our formulation treats time as relative: every generation step sees the same positional structure regardless of how far generation has progressed, and the state transition is identical at every chunk. Together, these properties introduce a recurrence into the generation process, where denoising serves as the transition function, and the KV cache serves as the carrier, requiring no external module. Experiments demonstrate that the adaptive state substantially improves video dynamics, enabling richer motion and natural scene progression within generated videos.

</details>


### [137] [VideoMLA: Low-Rank Latent KV Cache for Minute-Scale Autoregressive Video Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30351)
*Hidir Yesiltepe,Jiazhen Hu,Tuna Han Salih Meral,Adil Kaan Akan,Kaan Oktay,Hoda Eldardiry,Pinar Yanardag*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出VideoMLA，将视频扩散模型中每个注意力头的KV改为共享的低秩内容潜在表示与共享的解耦3D-RoPE位置键，KV缓存降至每层每token节省约92.7%，在长时序生成上质量与速度兼优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长序列视频扩散多采用固定大小滑窗KV缓存，但KV布局本身占主导内存与时延，基本未变；需要在不牺牲质量下显著压缩KV以提升长时序吞吐与可扩展性。

Method: 引入Multi-Head Latent Attention：用共享低秩内容潜在向量替代各头keys/values，并用共享解耦3D-RoPE作为位置键；分析为何在视频扩散中MLA有效，尽管预训练注意力谱并非低秩；通过实验表明有效秩由MLA瓶颈决定，光谱或随机初始化从起点就占满秩预算，训练在该预算内适配。

Result: - 每层每token KV内存减少92.7%。- 在VBench上：短时程与流式基线持平；长时程整体得分最佳；单卡B200吞吐提升约1.23倍。- 质量在高压缩比下仍保持，超出直接光谱近似的误差预测。

Conclusion: 改变KV布局为MLA能在不依赖真实低秩先验的前提下，大幅压缩KV并提升长时序视频扩散性能与吞吐；瓶颈本身决定有效秩，是比光谱低秩假设更实用的设计原则。

Abstract: Long-rollout causal video diffusion has converged on a fixed-size sliding-window KV cache, with recent progress innovating within this layout by changing which tokens occupy the window or how their positions are encoded. The per-head KV layout itself, a dominant contributor to streaming memory and latency, has been mostly left unchanged. In this paper, we present the first study of Multi-Head Latent Attention (MLA) in video diffusion. VideoMLA replaces per-head keys and values with a shared low-rank content latent and a shared decoupled 3D-RoPE positional key, reducing per-token KV memory by 92.7% at every cached layer. We further investigate why MLA succeeds in video diffusion even though the spectral assumption often used to motivate it in language models does not hold: pretrained video attention is not low-rank, with 99%-energy effective rank far above any practical latent dimension. VideoMLA retains quality at compression ratios where direct spectral approximation would predict large reconstruction error. We show that the MLA bottleneck, rather than the pretrained spectrum, determines the effective rank: both spectral and random initialization occupy nearly the full rank budget from initialization, and training preserves this budget while adapting within it. On VBench, VideoMLA matches short-horizon streaming video diffusion baselines, achieves the best overall score at long horizons among evaluated methods, and improves throughput by 1.23x on a single B200.

</details>


### [138] [GMOS: Grounding Moving Object Segmentation in 3D Space and Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30352)
*Junyu Xie,Tengda Han,Weidi Xie,Andrew Zisserman*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GMOS/GMOS-S：直接从RGB视频进行3D感知、时间细粒度的多运动目标分割与跟踪；并构建GMOS-2K数据集与MOS-I评测协议；在MOS、MOS-I与无监督VOS上达SOTA且更快，支持在线推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MOS依赖2D辅助模态（光流/轨迹）缺乏3D几何，且将“运动”视为序列级属性，忽视对象在任意时刻的瞬时运动状态；需要一个能在3D与时间维度上精确建模、无需离线2D先验、可高效在线推理的方案与评测标准。

Method: 1) 以3D与时间为基础：从原始RGB端到端学习，显式建模场景几何与对象瞬时运动。2) 框架GMOS：多对象、3D感知、时间细粒度分割与跟踪；以及轻量变体GMOS-S用于更快部署。3) 数据与协议：整理GMOS-2K（2210段真实视频），提供逐对象的时序运动标注；提出MOS-I评估协议，含三种互补指标以度量瞬时运动检测与分割质量。4) 训练/推理：支持在线流式推理，较少依赖离线预计算。

Result: GMOS在经典MOS、细粒度MOS-I以及无监督VOS基准上取得SOTA，同时相较以往多目标MOS方法显著加速，并能在线推理。

Conclusion: 通过在3D与时间维度上重构MOS定义与实现，GMOS/GMOS-S在精度与效率上均优于现有方法；GMOS-2K与MOS-I为社区提供了训练与公平评测瞬时运动分割的新基准与协议。

Abstract: Moving Object Segmentation (MOS) aims to discover, segment, and track objects that move independently of the camera. Current MOS methods, however, exhibit two fundamental limitations: they rely on pre-computed 2D auxiliary modalities such as optical flow or point trajectories that lack 3D geometric information, and they treat motion as a sequence-level attribute, overlooking the instantaneous motion state of each object. We address both by grounding MOS in 3D space and time, and propose GMOS, a framework that operates directly on RGB video to produce 3D-aware, temporally fine-grained segmentation of multiple moving objects, alongside a foreground--background variant GMOS-S for faster deployment. To support training and evaluation in this regime, we curate GMOS-2K, a dataset of 2,210 real-world videos with per-object temporal motion annotations drawn from five established Video Object Segmentation (VOS) benchmarks, and formalise MOS-I ("I" for instantaneous), a temporally fine-grained evaluation protocol with three complementary metrics. GMOS achieves state-of-the-art results across MOS, MOS-I, and Unsupervised VOS benchmarks, while running significantly faster than prior multi-object MOS methods and supporting online inference for streaming deployment.

</details>
